1. Murinzi We Vuz' Impanda
Written by W. J. Kirkpatrick

V1. Murinzi, jy' uvuz' impanda;
Uhan' umuntu wese.
Ng' uzumv' izo nkuru nziza,
Yihan' akizw' ibyaha

C. Murinzi we vuz' impanda!
Yivuze cyane hose (hose).
Menyesha bos' ubutumwa,
Imbohe zibohorwe.

V2. Yivugirize mu mpinga,
Mw' ishyamba mu gisiza;
Ndetse no mu nyanja hose,
Bameny' ako gakiza.

C. Murinzi we vuz' impanda!
Yivuze cyane hose (hose).
Menyesha bos' ubutumwa,
Imbohe zibohorwe.

V3. Yivugirize mu nzira,
Mu rwiherero hose.
Dat' arabategereje,
Nta cy' ataringanije.

C. Murinzi we vuz' impanda!
Yivuze cyane hose (hose).
Menyesha bos' ubutumwa,
Imbohe zibohorwe.

V4. Uyivugiriz' indembe,
Na zo zikizw' ibyaha.
Yes' arabatumir' ati:
Nimuze mbaboneze.

C. Murinzi we vuz' impanda!
Yivuze cyane hose (hose).
Menyesha bos' ubutumwa,
Imbohe zibohorwe.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

2. Umwam' Ageze Kw' irembo
Written by F. E. Belden

V1. Umwam' ageze kw' irembo,
Wabambwe ku musaraba;
Yaje gukorany' abera,
Babane mw' ijuru.

C. Kw' irembo (Kw' irembo),
Kw' irembo (Kw' irembo),
Kw' irembo, Ub' ari kw' irembo;
Nukw' araje (araje), Nukw' araje (araje),
Kand' ageze kw' irembo.

V2. Ibyerekana kuza kwe,
Birihuta kuboneka;
Kandi tugiye guhabwa,
Kubaho kw' iteka.

C. Kw' irembo (Kw' irembo),
Kw' irembo (Kw' irembo),
Kw' irembo, Ub' ari kw' irembo;
Nukw' araje (araje), Nukw' araje (araje),
Kand' ageze kw' irembo.

V3. Ntabw' intambar' izashira,
Ntabw' amahor' azahora,
Kerek' ibyaha n' urupfu,
Byatsembwe na Yesu.

C. Kw' irembo (Kw' irembo),
Kw' irembo (Kw' irembo),
Kw' irembo, Ub' ari kw' irembo;
Nukw' araje (araje), Nukw' araje (araje),
Kand' ageze kw' irembo.

V4. Maze mw' isi yagizwe nshya,
Niho tuzabahw' iteka;
Kudapfa kwakuye gupfa,
Dushiz' agahinda.

C. Kw' irembo (Kw' irembo),
Kw' irembo (Kw' irembo),
Kw' irembo, Ub' ari kw' irembo;
Nukw' araje (araje), Nukw' araje (araje),
Kand' ageze kw' irembo.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

3. Nzabona Yesu
Written by G. C. Tuller

V1. Nzabona Yesu mu maso,
Umuns' azatujyana;
Niho nzamwitegereza,
Kw' ari we wampfiriye.

C. Nzamurora mu maso ye,
Turi kumwe mw' ijuru;
Meny' uk' ubwiza bwe busa,
Nzamusingiz' iteka.

V2. Ubu ndamutekereza,
Ariko simurora;
Umuns' uhiriw' uzaza,
Nzamubonan' ubwiza.

C. Nzamurora mu maso ye,
Turi kumwe mw' ijuru;
Meny' uk' ubwiza bwe busa,
Nzamusingiz' iteka.

V3. Tuzishimir' imbere ye,
Ubw' ishavu rishize;
Ibigande, biganduwe,
N' ahijimye hakeye.

C. Nzamurora mu maso ye,
Turi kumwe mw' ijuru;
Meny' uk' ubwiza bwe busa,
Nzamusingiz' iteka.

V4. Nzanezererw' imbere ye,
Nzamurora mumenye;
Nzabana na Yes' unkunda,
Niwe Mukiza wanjye.

C. Nzamurora mu maso ye,
Turi kumwe mw' ijuru;
Meny' uk' ubwiza bwe busa,
Nzamusingiz' iteka.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

4. Har' Amakuru Meza
Written by Unknown

V1. Har' amakuru mez' amenywa n' abagenzi,
Bazerera kure y' iwabo,
Kuk' Umukiz' agiye kuza mu bwiza bwe,
Kand' agiye kwim' ingoma ye.

C. Azaza, ndabizi kw' azagaruka,
Nukw' azaza rwos' azaza.
Abagenzi bose barembye,
Bazakir' Umukiza n' aza kwima.

V2. Ibituro by' abera bos' uko bangana,
Byose bizakingurwa rwose;
Kand' inteko z' abasinzira mu kuzimu,
Bazongera gutura kw' isi.

C. Azaza, ndabizi kw' azagaruka,
Nukw' azaza rwos' azaza.
Abagenzi bose barembye,
Bazakir' Umukiza n' aza kwima.

V3. Nta kizadutanya mur' iyo si nshya nziza,
Tuzaririmb' uko twakize.
Abacunguwe bazaba bavuye hose,
Baramy' Umwami wo mw' ijuru.

C. Azaza, ndabizi kw' azagaruka,
Nukw' azaza rwos' azaza.
Abagenzi bose barembye,
Bazakir' Umukiza n' aza kwima.

V4. Haleluy' amina, haleluya iteka;
Nitwitonda tuzahatura.
Ba maso nezerwa, kand' ujye wiringira;
Maz' uzambar' ikamba ryiza.

C. Azaza, ndabizi kw' azagaruka,
Nukw' azaza rwos' azaza.
Abagenzi bose barembye,
Bazakir' Umukiza n' aza kwima.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

5. Murinzi We Menyesh' Igihe
Written by Unknown

V1. Murinzi we! menyesh' igihe!
Mbes' iwacu n' imuhero?
At' ijoro ryijimye cyane,
Ariko buracya.
Ntukarire, Gumy' ugende,
Nturorere kwiringira,
Kugez' igih' uzasohora,
Mu muns' uhoraho.

V2. Murwanyi we! Tyo mbwira nawe!
Ansubiza yitonz' ati:
Intambar' igiye gushira.
Guma ku rugamba.
Wibabara, ihangane,
Wirek' imirimo yawe,
Kuko tuzabon' ibihembo,
Tumaze gutsinda.

V3. Ndacyabaz' ibyaremwe byose,
Binsubiza bitya biti:
Iy' is' igiye guhanguka.
Haz' ind' idashira.
Ntukarir' ibimenyetso,
Byerekan' aho tugeze,
Kand' ibintu byose byaremwe,
Biriteg' impanda.

V4. Imuhir' ubu ni bugufi,
Tunezerwe mu mitima.
Duhumure ko tuzakira,
Dushir' agahinda.
Ntukarire tuzabana,
Amakub' azab' ashize.
Ntabwo tuzabur' amahoro
Mu rugo rwa Data.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

6. Mwebw' Abera Mube Maso
Written by  W. J. Kirkpatrick

V1. Mwebw' abera mube maso, 
Ibyaremwe birahinda.
Mukomez' imuri zanyu, 
Mwiteg' Umwam' ari hafi.

C. Araje Yes' araje! 
Azanye n' icyubahiro.
Yes' aje kwim' ingoma Ye, 
Araje, Yes' araje.

V2. Wibuk' Umuvunyi wawe, 
Agakiza n' imbabazi,
Ikamba, icyubahiro. 
Jya wogez' ako gakiza.

C. Araje Yes' araje! 
Azanye n' icyubahiro.
Yes' aje kwim' ingoma Ye, 
Araje, Yes' araje.

V3. Nta bwami budahanguka; 
Wumv' amagare y' asuma.
Bwira bos' iby' imbabazi, 
Ubu n' igihe cy' impuhwe.

C. Araje Yes' araje! 
Azanye n' icyubahiro.
Yes' aje kwim' ingoma Ye, 
Araje, Yes' araje.

V4. Amoko yos' azashira; 
Krist' atebuts' ubwami bwe;
Is' igiye guhanguka; 
Nimwishim' abahiriwe.

C. Araje Yes' araje! 
Azanye n' icyubahiro.
Yes' aje kwim' ingoma Ye, 
Araje, Yes' araje.

V5. Banyabyaha mwe nimuze! 
Abitwarire kuri Se.
Mwese nimugire bwangu! 
Imbabazi zikiriho.

C. Araje Yes' araje! 
Azanye n' icyubahiro.
Yes' aje kwim' ingoma Ye, 
Araje, Yes' araje.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

7. Ubwo Yesu Azagaruka
Written by G. F. Root

V1. Ubwo Yes' azagaruka, 
Kujyan' abe bose,
Bemeye kumuyoboka, 
N' abatoni be.

C. Bazaka nk' inyenyeri, 
Zitatse kw' ikamba rye;
Bazatangaza cyane, 
Bakize rwose.

V2. Ubw' azaza gukorany' 
abo yatoye bose,
Bera baboneye rwose, 
B' abatoni be.

C. Bazaka nk' inyenyeri, 
Zitatse kw' ikamba rye;
Bazatangaza cyane, 
Bakize rwose.

V3. Yemwe bana! Yemwe bana! 
Bakund' Umukiza;
Abakunda, abakunda, 
Nk' abatoni be.

C. Bazaka nk' inyenyeri, 
Zitatse kw' ikamba rye;
Bazatangaza cyane, 
Bakize rwose.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

8. Abarokots'Ibyago Byo Hasi.
Written by J. M. Black

V1. Abarokots' ibyago byo hasi bazakoranywa,
Ab' azatumir' azajyana na bo.
Umwami n' agaruk' ikondera rye rizavuga,
Amatek' azab' agiye gucibwa.

C. Azaba yabararitse,
Ubw' azabahamagara.
Azaba yabararitse,
Ab' azatumir' azajyana nabo.

V2. Uwo muns' abapfuye muri Kristo bazazurwa,
Bazava mu bituro nka we rwose.
Abo yitoreye bazimana nawe mw' ijuru,
Ubw' azagenda, azajyana na bo.

C. Azaba yabararitse,
Ubw' azabahamagara.
Azaba yabararitse,
Ab' azatumir' azajyana nabo.

V3. Niho tuzajya dukorer' Umwami tudahwema;
Tuzajya dusingiz' urukundo rwe.
Maz' ubwo tuzarangiz' imirimo yacu mw' isi,
Tuzateranywa tujyanwe mw' ijuru.

C. Azaba yabararitse,
Ubw' azabahamagara.
Azaba yabararitse,
Ab' azatumir' azajyana nabo.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

9. Vuz' Impanda Yumvikane Hose
Written by G. E. Lee

V1. Vuz' impanda yumvikane hose, 
Yesu agiye kuza!
Muririmbe bagenzi mwishima, 
Yesu agiye kuza.

C. Ari hafi, Ari hafi,
Umwam' agiye kuza.

V2. Mujye muhererekanya hose, 
Yesu agiye kuza!
Azazan' icyubahiro cyinshi, 
Yesu agiye kuza.

C. Ari hafi, Ari hafi,
Umwam' agiye kuza.

V3. Yivugirize mu nyanja hose, 
Yesu agiye kuza!
Yivugirize no mu bikombe, 
Yesu agiye kuza.

C. Ari hafi, Ari hafi,
Umwam' agiye kuza.

V4. Mu misoz' uyihavugirize, 
Yesu agiye kuza!
Imiyag' ijyan' ayo makuru, 
Yesu agiye kuza.

C. Ari hafi, Ari hafi,
Umwam' agiye kuza.

V5. Amok' ubw' azasubiranamo, 
Yesu agiye kuza!
Ubwenge bwungukwa bwerekana, 
Ko Yes' agiye kuza.

C. Ari hafi, Ari hafi,
Umwam' agiye kuza.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

10. Duhurire Ku Mugezi
Written by Rev. R. Lowry

V1. Duhurire ku mugezi,
Dusang' abamarayika;
Amazi yaw' atunganye,
Atemb' av' imbere y' Imana.

C. Nuko tujye ku mugezi!
Duhurire n' abera ku mugezi!
Ku mugez' utunganye w' Imana,
Utemb' imbere y' intebe.

V2. Ku nkombe y' uwo mugezi,
Ni ho tuzatambagira,
Turamy' Umwami w' Iteka,
Mu gihe cyiza kidashira.

C. Nuko tujye ku mugezi!
Duhurire n' abera ku mugezi!
Ku mugez' utunganye w' Imana,
Utemb' imbere y' intebe.

V3. Tuzagera ku mugezi,
Dutur' imitwaro yacu;
Tuzakirishw' imbabazi,
Duhabw' umwambaro n' ikamba.

C. Nuko tujye ku mugezi!
Duhurire n' abera ku mugezi!
Ku mugez' utunganye w' Imana,
Utemb' imbere y' intebe.

V4. Ub' umugez' uri hafi,
Urugendo ruzashira;
Tuzishima mu mitima,
N' indirimbo z' umunezero.

C. Nuko tujye ku mugezi!
Duhurire n' abera ku mugezi!
Ku mugez' utunganye w' Imana,
Utemb' imbere y' intebe.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

11. Mukiza Ngukurikire
Written by J.Lawson

V1. Mukiza ngukurikire, 
Ah' unshakira hose;
Ah' ujya ngukurikire, 
Mwami ngukurikire.

C. Mukiza ngukurikire, 
Wamviriy' amaraso;
Nib' utagir' ukwitaho, 
Jye nkwikurikirire.

V2. Nahw' inzira yazitirwa, 
Naho yakukumuka,
Ko wayinyuzemo mbere, 
Nyicamo mfit' ishimwe.

C. Mukiza ngukurikire, 
Wamviriy' amaraso;
Nib' utagir' ukwitaho, 
Jye nkwikurikirire.

V3. Naho naterwa n' ibyago, 
Nkageragezwa cyane,
Warageragejwe nawe, 
Mwami ngukurikize.

C. Mukiza ngukurikire, 
Wamviriy' amaraso;
Nib' utagir' ukwitaho, 
Jye nkwikurikirire.

V4. Nib' unyobora mw' ishavu, 
Niba nkena nkanenwa,
Wigeze kuba ruvumwa, 
Nanjye ngukurikize.

C. Mukiza ngukurikire, 
Wamviriy' amaraso;
Nib' utagir' ukwitaho, 
Jye nkwikurikirire.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

12. Har' Isoko
Written by Unknown

V1. Har' isokw' ivamw' amaraso,
Yo mu mitsi y' Imanuweri.
Ni y' atungany' abanyabyaha,
Bagashirahw' inenge,
Bag' atsembwahw' ibicumuro,
Byose bikabacikaho.
Niy' atungany' abanyabyaha,
Bagashirahw' inenge.

V2. Igisambo ku musaraba,
Kiyarabutswe cyarihannye;
Nanjye mbwiriza nkwizigire,
Noye kujya nshumura;
Ibyaha mbicikeho rwose,
Noye kujya nkugomera;
Nanjye mbwiriza nkwizigire,
Noye kujya nshumura.

V3. Amaraso yaw' atunganye,
Ahoran' imbaraga nyinshi;
Niyo wacunguj' itorero,
Aritsembamw' ibyaha;
Ryaganjij' imbaraga yabyo.
Ryarabirokotse rwose.
Niyo wacunguj' itorero,
Yaritsembyemw' ibyaha.

V4. Mperey' igihe meny' isoko,
Iva mu bikomere byawe.
Nogez' urwo rukundo rwawe,
Nzahora ngusingiza;
Nzahora ngusingiz' iteka,
Nzajya ngusingiz' iteka.
Nogez' urwo rukundo rwawe,
Nzahora ngusingiza.

V5. Mwami mpora ngucumuraho,
Mpa kwizer' imbabazi zawe!
N' amaraso yaw' atunganye,
Mpa kuramishwa nawe!
Mpa kuramishwa nawe Yesu!
Mpa no kuramishwa nawe!
N' amaraso yaw' atunganye,
Mpa kuramishwa nawe!

V6. Har' indirimbo zera ntazi,
Nzaziririmbira mw' ijuru.
Naho nagobw' ururim' ubu,
Uzarugobotora;
Uzarugobotora Yesu,
Ni wow' uzankiza rwose.
Naho nagobw' ururim' ubu,
Uzarugobotora.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

13. Mwami Yesu Ndifuza
Written by  W. J. Kirkpatrick

V1. Mwami Yesu ndifuza k' umboneza;
Ndashaka k' umba mu mutim' iteka.
Noye kujya nita ku bigirwamana.
Umboneze rwose nere ndush' ingwa.

C. Ngo nere de ndush' urubura!
Mpa kwer' ubu ngutunganire rwose!

V2. Mwami jy' undebera ku ntebe yawe!
Mpa gutamb' igitambo kiboneye!
Ndeke gushidikanya nitange rwose.
Umboneze rwose nere ndush' ingwa.

C. Ngo nere de ndush' urubura!
Mpa kwer' ubu ngutunganire rwose!

V3. Yesu ndagutakambira nkomeje!
Ngo mbon' uko nkwitega Mwami mwiza!
Ntunganish' umuvu w' amaraso yawe!
Umboneze rwose nere ndush' ingwa.

C. Ngo nere de ndush' urubura!
Mpa kwer' ubu ngutunganire rwose!

V4. Mwami ngutegereje nihanganye,
Yesu ngwin' ump' umutim' utunganye!
Ntiwari wirengagiz' abagushaka.
Umboneze rwose nere ndush' ingwa.

C. Ngo nere de ndush' urubura!
Mpa kwer' ubu ngutunganire rwose!

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

agwa, agwa, 
amatur' agwa;
Yose n' aya Yesu,

ryo mu twana twe.

agwa, agwa, 
amatur' agwa;

agwa, agwa, 
amatur' agwa;

C. Agwa, agwa, 
agwa, agwa,

15. Urukundo Rwa Yesu
Written by W. B. Bradbury

V1. Urukundo rwa Yesu, 
Rwageze kuri twebwe;
Rudukuraho rwose, 
Urubanza rwo gupfa.

C. Aradukunda, aradukunda,
Aradukunda, Yesu Mutabazi.

V2. Abatari bahabwa, 
Ubugingo bw' iteka,
Twihute tubabwire, 
Urukundo rwa Yesu.

C. Aradukunda, aradukunda,
Aradukunda, Yesu Mutabazi.

V3. Kuko yaradukunze, 
Yadupfiriye twese,
Natwe dukunde dutyo, 
Abakiri mu byaha.

C. Aradukunda, aradukunda,
Aradukunda, Yesu Mutabazi.

V4. Aho Yes' azazira, 
Aje kwim' ingoma ye,
Ni bwo tuzumv' ijwi rye, 
Ati: Mwakoze neza.

C. Aradukunda, aradukunda,
Aradukunda, Yesu Mutabazi.

V5. Akir' uyu mutima, 
Weze maz' ub' uwawe,
Wambabwiwe ku giti, 
Nzagukunda mb' uwawe.

C. Aradukunda, aradukunda,
Aradukunda, Yesu Mutabazi.

V3. Mpang' amabokw' amaso,

C. Nitondesh' intambwe, 
Aho njya hose.

17. Njye Nsingiz' Urukundo

Ni rwo rumbwiriza,

Bakamenya Yesu.

Bakamenya Yesu.

bamw' ibwami bwawe.

Data We ngukurikize!

Bakamenya Yesu.

V3. Maz' ibyo ni bishira, 
Tuzabe mw' ijuru,

Mwami w' urukundo.

C. Data We ko nd' umwana wawe!
Data We ngukurikize!

Bakamenya Yesu.

18. Yemwe Ngabo Z' Umwami
Written by Sir A. Sillivan

V1. Yemwe ngabo z' Umwami! Nimutabare!
Tujyane na Yesu! Niw' utabaza.
Twitwaz' umusaraba! utujy' imbere!
Mwese nimuze tugabe! Tunesh' Umwanzi.

C. Yemwe ngabo z' Umwami mwese!
Dutabare twese! Tujyane na Yesu!
Dutsind' Umwanzi.

V2. Ababisha bahunga, Babony' intwari.
Nimuze tuneshe, Ngabo z' Umwami!
Intangiriro z' isi zinyeganyezwa,
N' ibyishimo by' ab' Umwami, bamusingiza.

C. Yemwe ngabo z' Umwami mwese!
Dutabare twese! Tujyane na Yesu!
Dutsind' Umwanzi.

V3. Itorero ry' Imana, Rirafatanya;
Rirahaguruka, kunesh' Umwanzi.
Nta kizaduteranya, Turakundana,
Duhora duhuj' inama, Twizera kimwe.

C. Yemwe ngabo z' Umwami mwese!
Dutabare twese! Tujyane na Yesu!
Dutsind' Umwanzi.

V1. Mwami, nzi kw' ari we nkunda, 
kurut' iby' iyi si;
Kuko wampay' amahoro 
atagir' impinduka.

C. Urukundo rwankijije (ngakira) 
ntirurondoreka.
Ntitwarusobanukirwa (na hato) 
kuko ruhebuje.

V2. Nzi k' uhor' unzirikana, 
undutira byose.
Mwami, kugutekereza 
bindutir' ibyiratwa.

C. Urukundo rwankijije (ngakira) 
ntirurondoreka.
Ntitwarusobanukirwa (na hato) 
kuko ruhebuje.

V3. Wanyujuj' umunezero, 
natay' umuruho.
Kumenya k' Unkunda cyane, 
ni byo bimpumuriza.

C. Urukundo rwankijije (ngakira) 
ntirurondoreka.
Ntitwarusobanukirwa (na hato) 
kuko ruhebuje.

V4. Mucunguzi wanjye mwiza, 
icyakunyereka!
Ngo tuzabane my ijuru, 
ahatab' agahinda.

C. Urukundo rwankijije (ngakira) 
ntirurondoreka.
Ntitwarusobanukirwa (na hato) 
kuko ruhebuje.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

136. Ahw' Azanyobora Hose
Written by J. M. Black

V1. Ahw' azanyobora hose, 
ni ho nzishimira kujya;
Kukw' ari jye yapfiriye, 
akanzir' atacumuye.

C. Yes' azanyobor' iteka, 
maz' angez' i w' amahoro;
Kukw' ar' inshuti y' ukuri, 
itigeze guhemuka.

V2. Nishimira kw' antegeka, 
nishimira kw' anyobora.
Nishimira kumwumvira, 
kukw' ari jye yapfiriye.

C. Yes' azanyobor' iteka, 
maz' angez' i w' amahoro;
Kukw' ar' inshuti y' ukuri, 
itigeze guhemuka.

V3. Singishidikanya rwose, 
kuko ndi kumwe na Yesu.
Nizigiye ko vub' aha, 
nzamureba duhanganye.

C. Yes' azanyobor' iteka, 
maz' angez' i w' amahoro;
Kukw' ar' inshuti y' ukuri, 
itigeze guhemuka.

V1. Isi ndayihararutse,

C. Imbabazi zidashira 
n' urukundo rw' iteka,
Ni byo bijya binyemeza 
ko nzaramishwa nawe.

V2. Isi ndayihararutse, 
mpisemo Yesu gusa.
Mu kaga ni we humure; 
nzahora nezerewe.

C. Imbabazi zidashira

Ni byo bijya binyemeza 
ko nzaramishwa nawe.

ko nzaramishwa nawe.

V4. Isi ndayihararutse, 
mpisemo Yesu gusa.
Nzirat' umusaraba we, 
yatangiyeho kera.

C. Imbabazi zidashira

ko nzaramishwa nawe.

138. Mwami Wanjye, Nyakira
Written by W. J. Kirkpatrick

V1. Mwami wanjye nyakira, 
ndakwiyeguriy' ubu;
Ngay' amaboko yanjye; 
yakoresh' uk' ushaka.

C. Nyuhagiz' amaraso yawe (nere rwose) ;
Maz' anyezehw' inenge yose (nere rwose) ;
Ibyanjye byose ndabikweguriye, 
none n' iteka ryose.

V2. Ngib' ibirenge byanjye, 
byerekez' ah' ushaka.
Ngir' ijwi ryanjye na ryo, 
rijye riguhimbaza.

C. Nyuhagiz' amaraso yawe (nere rwose) ;
Maz' anyezehw' inenge yose (nere rwose) ;
Ibyanjye byose ndabikweguriye, 
none n' iteka ryose.

V3. Nguhay' akanwa kanjye; 
Mwami, kakuvugire.
Ngub' ubutunzi bwanjye, 
sinzagir' icyo nkwima.

C. Nyuhagiz' amaraso yawe (nere rwose) ;
Maz' anyezehw' inenge yose (nere rwose) ;
Ibyanjye byose ndabikweguriye, 
none n' iteka ryose.

V4. Nguhay' igihe cyanjye, 
sinzakiguteraho;
Nguhay' ubwenge bwanjye; 
bukoresh' uk' ushaka.

C. Nyuhagiz' amaraso yawe (nere rwose) ;
Maz' anyezehw' inenge yose (nere rwose) ;
Ibyanjye byose ndabikweguriye, 
none n' iteka ryose.

V5. Ngiy' imigambi yanjye; 
igengwe nawe, Mwami.
Nguy' umutima wanjye, 
ub' uwawe rwose.

C. Nyuhagiz' amaraso yawe (nere rwose) ;
Maz' anyezehw' inenge yose (nere rwose) ;
Ibyanjye byose ndabikweguriye, 
none n' iteka ryose.

V6. Mwam' urukundo rwanjye 
ni wowe nzarukunda;
Nkwihaye nimazeyo, 
none n' iteka ryose.

C. Nyuhagiz' amaraso yawe (nere rwose) ;
Maz' anyezehw' inenge yose (nere rwose) ;
Ibyanjye byose ndabikweguriye, 
none n' iteka ryose.

139. Nahony' Inshut' Ihebuje
Written by G. C. Stebbins

V1. Nabony' inshut' ihebuje! Yankunze ntarabaho;
Yanyiyegereshej' ineza n' urukundo rw' iteka,
Bituma dushyikirana ubudatandukana;
Kuko nd' uwe, nawe n' uwanjye, ibihe bidashira.

V2. Nabony' inshut' ihebuje! Yamberey' impongano.
Urets' ibyo kump' ubugingo, yaranyitangiriye.
Nta cyo mfite nit' icyanjye, kuko tubisangiye.
Ndamwiyeguriye burundu; ibihe bidashira.

V3. Nabony' inshut' ihebuje! Nyir' ubutware bwose!
Ni bw' indindish' uko bukeye; izangeza mw' ijuru.
Ibyiza byanshyizw' imbere binsubizamw' intege;
Reka nkore, noye kwiganda, ngez' ubw' izanduhura.

V4. Nabony' inshut' ihebuje! y' impuhwe n' urukundo.
Ni y' indind' ikanyunganira; ni y' indenger' iteka.
Mbese n' iki cyadutanya, ko dukundana rwose?
N' iby' iyi si, cyangwa s' urupfu ? Oya, nzab' uw' iteka.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

az' azakubeshaho, unyw' uram' iteka.

Nshir' inyota, ndahembuka; nzahorana na we.

V3. Numvise Yes' ambwir' ati: Ni jye Mucyo w' isi.
N' undeb' uramurikirwa, ntuzarindagira.
Maze muhanz' amaso koko, mbon' ar' izuba ryanjye;
Rizamvir' iminsi yose y' ubugingo bwanjye.

Written by S. Wesley

V1. Yes' Umwami w' abami, ngwin' ube muri jye!
He kub' ari jy' uvuga, ujy' umvugiramo.

Maz' abajya bandeba, bajye bakubona.

V2. Ndakwiyeguriy' ubu, ez' ibyaha byanjye;
Ngaragareh' ubwiza bwawe buhebuje.

Niyoroshye nganduke, ngo nkoreshwe nawe.

V3. Ingingo zanjye zose zijye zikumvira;
Uzikoreshereze zikubahirize.

Y' ibimbaho, nishama, nta mahoro mfite.

V4. Ni wowe ntegereje, ungenz' uk' ushaka.
Ubwanjye nditeguye, simfit' ikinziga.
Yes' Umwami w' abami, ngwin' ube muri jye!
Maz' ibyo nkora byose, mbikoreshwe nawe.

Aho njyanye na Yesu mb' amahoro.

C. Aho njyanye nawe, nta kintinyisha,
Aho njyanye na Yesu mb' amahoro.

Written by G. F. Root

Bo gusarur' abakiranutsi?
Babangir' ukuri nk' imihoro,
Kandi ntibab' ar' abanyabute.

C. Abasaruzi se bari he?
Ngo bafatanye natwe gusarura,
Maze twishime, turi kumwe,
Isarura ni rirangira

V2. Mushakire mu mihana yose;

Isarura ni rirangira

Umurimo wab' urabasaze.

C. Abasaruzi se bari he?
Ngo bafatanye natwe gusarura,
Maze twishime, turi kumwe,
Isarura ni rirangira

V4. Mwa bantu mwe, mwahur' imihoro!
Musarur' igihe kirageze!

Dor' abazaniy' ingororano!

C. Abasaruzi se bari he?
Ngo bafatanye natwe gusarura,

Isarura ni rirangira

152. Ngwino Yesu
Written by Adapted by L. L. Pickett

V1. Ngwino Yes' uvugane n' umutima wanjye:
Maz' umpumuriz' uti:Nta bwo nagusize.
Nyugurur' umutima, nihutire kumva
Ijwi ryawe ry' impuhwe, nyuzuz' ibyishimo.

C. Mbwiz' ijwi ryongorera, mbwiran' urukundo;
Ut' Uzanesh' iteka, ub' umudendezo.
Vugana nanjy' iteka, mbwir' ubudahwema;
Reka numv' uk' umbwira ngo: Sinaguhanye.

V2. Yobora abana bawe, uvugane na bo;
Ubuzuz' ibyishimo, bige kugusenga.
Mwami, bitange rwose, bakwiyegurire;
Tebuts' ubwami bwawe, twibanire nawe.

C. Mbwiz' ijwi ryongorera, mbwiran' urukundo;
Ut' Uzanesh' iteka, ub' umudendezo.
Vugana nanjy' iteka, mbwir' ubudahwema;
Reka numv' uk' umbwira ngo: Sinaguhanye.

V3. Ngwin' uvugane natwe, uduhishurire
Iby' imigambi yawe, n' inshingano yacu.
Duhe kuguhimbaza, tukubahirize,
Tujye tunezererwa gukor' iby' ushaka.

C. Mbwiz' ijwi ryongorera, mbwiran' urukundo;
Ut' Uzanesh' iteka, ub' umudendezo.
Vugana nanjy' iteka, mbwir' ubudahwema;
Reka numv' uk' umbwira ngo: Sinaguhanye.

153. Mwami, Sinsabir' Iby' Ejo
Written by F. E. Belden

V1. Mwami, sinsabir' iby' ejo; mfasha none,
Ndind' urukongi rw' ibyaha, uyu munsi.
Ne gucumuz' ururimi, mputiyeho;
Mwami, rind' iminwa yanjye, uyu munsi.

V2. Njye nshunguz' ubury' umwete, no gusenga;
Ngwe neza mu buryo bwose, uyu munsi.
Nkomeze nkor' iby' ushaka, ngire bwangu;

asezerano yawe, ndayiteze;
Mwami, sinsabir' iby' ejo, mfasha none;
Ndind' unkomez' undagire, uyu munsi; en.

154. Murinzi We, Ngaho Mbwira
Written by W. B. Bradbury

V1. Murinzi we, ngaho mbwira, mbese bugiye gucya?
Nta bimenyets' urabona, k' Umwami yegereje?
Mugenzi we haguruka! Umusek' uratambitse;
Tyo kenyera, maz' ukeshe, haguruka; bwakeye!

V2. Murinzi we, dor' umucyo ukomeje gukwira!
Reba naw' ibimenyetso, bitangaza kuza kwe.
Ubw' impanda zizavuga, abapfuye bazazuka
Ubutazongera gupfa, bibanire n'Umwami.

V3. Murinzi we, vuz' impundu, igihe kirageze!
Mwese, nimurangurure, mubyamamaze hose.
Mugenzi we, nawe reba; ubwami bugeze hafi;
Ngiriya Yerusalemu irarabagirana.

V4. Murinzi, mur' uwo murwa, w' igikundiro rwose,
Ni h' Umwami w' i Sioni adutegerereje.
Ubwami bwe buragutse, buhetuy' iyi si yose;
N' ubwami budahanguka; hahirw' ababujyamo.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

155. Aho Nzahamagaiwa Hose
Written by C. E. Rounsefell

V1. Aho nzahamagarwa hose, ari no mu misozi,
Cyangwa ku rugamba rukaze; Mubyeyi, n' unkenera,
Ukambwiz' ijwi ryawe ritoya,
Ukanyuz' inzira ntazi,
Nzakwishyira mu maboko, mvuge nti:
Nzajy' ah' unshakira hose.

C. Nzajy' ah' unshakira hose, Mwami;
Mu misozi no mu bibaya.
Nzavug' iby' ushaka ko mvuga Mwami,
Kandi nzaba nk' uk' ushaka.

V2. Ahari Yes' ashaka yuko muvugir' uyu munsi;
Ahari babonek' impabe, nkwiriye guhabura;
Murokozi wanjye, n' unyobora,
N' ahar' ibihanamanga;
Sinzareka kogez' inkuru yawe;
Nzajy' ah' unshakira hose.

C. Nzajy' ah' unshakira hose, Mwami;
Mu misozi no mu bibaya.
Nzavug' iby' ushaka ko mvuga Mwami,
Kandi nzaba nk' uk' ushaka.

V3. Nta bwo nshidikanya, har' aho Mwam' ushaka ko nkora.
Mu kubaho kwanjye kugufi, nkorer' Uwambambiwe.
Mwami, nkubikij' ibyanjye hyose,
Nzi k' unkunda bitangaje.
Nzakor' iby' ushaka, mhikunze cyane;
Nzajy' ah' unshakira hose.

C. Nzajy' ah' unshakira hose, Mwami;
Mu misozi no mu bibaya.
Nzavug' iby' ushaka ko mvuga Mwami,
Kandi nzaba nk' uk' ushaka.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

156. Amagambo Y' Umujmya
Written by H. R. Palmer

V1. Amagambo y' umujinya, ntakabave mu kanwa !
Ahubw' umutim' uyacuby' atararushy' asohoka.

C. S. na A.: Mukundane rwose; Yes' aravug' ati:
Ngiri tegeko ryanjye mbahaye: Mukundane rwose,
Yes' aravug' ati: Bana banjye, mukundane.
T. na B.: Mukundane, mukundane ; ngiri tegeko ryanjye:
Mukundane, mukundane; n' itegeko rye.

V2. Urukundo n' imbonera, n' ubucuti, birera;
Byab' ishyano kubyicisha ubupfu bw' akanya gato.

V3. Amagambo y' intonganya ntaregama mu kanwa,
Ijambo rimwe ry' intonganya ritandukany' inshuti.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

157. N' Igihe Cy' Isarura
Written by C. S. Cable

V1. Nib' umunt' agend' abiba, asohoy' imbuto nziza,
Ntacogora ngw' agw' isari, ahirwa n'Uwiteka.

C. Yemwe ga ngo zirakura! Reba naw' uko zingana!
Imirima yos' ireze, n' igihe cy' isarura.

V2. Ikime kiva mw' ijuru, n' umucy' urabagirana
Bizatum' imbuto zera, kubw' ubuntu bw' Imana.

V3. Bib' imbuto, wicogora; woye gukuk' umutima.
N' ubw' iby' ubon' ar' umwaku, uzasarur' ishimwe.

158. Isarura Ry' Isi Riregereje

V1. Isarura ry' isi riregereje,
Yes' arahamagar' abasaruzi.

Nimuzan' imihoro musarure!

C. S. na A.: Mugire bwangu, muhunik' imiba;
Mugire bwangu, nimuze.
T. na B.: Mugire bwangu mwese;
Nimuze, muhunik' imiba Ye.

V2. Uwo muns' utazabamw' amarira,
Uhora wegerej' uko bukeye.
Imyaka yararitswe n' umuyaga,
Mugire bwangw' imvur' itarahanguka.

V3. Urukundo ni nk' isokw' idakama,
Ituruka mw' ijuru ku Muremyi;
Ni rwo ruturarikira gukora,

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

V1. Nyabun' uburyo ngukennye!,
Nd' umukene n' impumyi;
Mfat' ukubok' unyobore,
Ni wow' ump' imbaraga.

C. Ku manywa na n' ijoro;
Mwami ndagushak' iteka;
Ku manywa na n' ijoro;
Mwam' unyikomereze.

V2. Nyambik' urukundo rwawe,
Nahindanye nd' intebyi.
Ubu mfit' intege nkeya,
Nyongeramw' imbaraga.

V3. Nzab' amahor' unyoboye,
Sinakwiyiringira.
Yes' ujy' ungend' i ruhande,
Kuk' undutira byose.

V4. Nubw' ibind' imbere byose
Byankoma mu nkokora,
Nzakomeza komatana nawe,
Mwana w' Imana.

Written by I. D. Sankey
V1. Icyampa nkab' uwawe, Yes' Umwami wanjye;

Jye nta cyo maze, nta cyo, nta cyo;
Ni We mpay' ikuzo.

V2. Icyampa nkab' uwawe, Yes' Umwami wanjye.
Nkoresh' uk' ushaka, njye nkubahiriza.

V3. Icyampa nkab' uwawe, Yes' Umwami wanjye;

V4. Icyampa nkab' uwawe, Yes' Umwami wanjye;

161. Mfit' lnshuti Y' Ukuri
Written by H. P. Main

V1. Mfit' inshuti y' ukuri, y' inkoramutima;
Irankunda bihebuje, nzi kw' itazampana.
Nta bwo nayiv' i ruhande, nkunda ko tubana,
Iyo nshuti ni Yesu, Umukiza.

V2. Iyo nguy' agacuho, ameny' uko meze;
Ntanyirengagiza rwose: aransindagiza,
Akanyobora mu nzira yo gukiranuka;
N' inshuti nkunda cyane, Yes' Umwami.

V3. Mutur' umubabaro, mubwir' ibyishimo;
Mubwir' ibinyura na byo, n' ibindushya byose.
Angaragariz' uburyo nkwiriye kwifata;
Nkunda kwiganirira na w' iteka.

V4. Az' imigambi yanjye yo gukiz' abandi;
Ni ko kunshing' umurimo wo kumuvugira,
No kwamamaz' urukundo, rwatumy' adupfira:
Yewe, mukunda rwose, bihebuje.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

162. Umukiz' Aranyobora
Written by Rev. R. Lowry

V1. Umukiz' aranyobora, birampagije rwose.
Sinshidikany' impuhwe ze,
Kuko njya nzibonaho.
ahoro yo mw' ijuru yanyuzuy' umutima;
Sinzatinya na hatoya, kuko Yes' anyobora;
Sinzatinyana hatoya, kuko Yes' anyobora.

V2. Umukiz' aranyobora, akanampumuriza;
Iyo ngeze mu makuba, ntamvirira na hato;
Bona nubwo nateguza, yandamir' akamfasha;
Ahor' anyitahw' iteka, nta cyo nzamuburana;
Ahor' anyitahw' iteka, nta cyo nzamuburana.

V3. Umukiz' aranyobora, ni ryo humure ryanjye!
Ni w' uzampaz' uburame; njye mpora muhimbaza.
Nta cyatuma ntiny' urupfu, mfit' iryo sezerano;
Nzajya ndirimb' iteka, nti: Yesu ni w' unyobora;
Nzajya ndirimb' iteka, nti: Yesu ni w' unyobora.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

163. Yes' Arahamagar' ati:
Written by F. E. Belden

V1. Yes' arahamagar' ati: Ni nd' unkorera none?
Isarura rirageze, ni nd' uribusarure?
Umv' ukw' aduhamagara; kand' azagororera
Umusubiza wes' ati: Ndi hano Mwami ntuma.

V2. N' utabasha kujya kure, ngo wambuke n' inyanja;
N' ino har' abapagani, wagarurira Yesu.
N' utabasha gushyanuka, ngo wigishe nka Paulo,
Wakogez' iby' urukundo rw'Umukiza wabambwe.

V3. Wabura kub' umurinzi, ku nkike z' i Sioni,
Wafashish' amashengesho, no gutur' amaturo;
Ukayobora n' abandi, mu nzir' ijya mw' ijuru,
Nk' ukw' Aroni yakomeje amaboko ya Mose.

V4. Abantu bari mu kaga; Yes' aragutabaza.
Ntukagir' ubw' uvug' uti: Nta cyo nakora rwose.
Ishimire gukoreshwa, hitamw' umurimo we;
Maz' usubize bwang' uti: Ndi hano, Mwami ntuma.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

164. Nicay' Imbere Ya Yesu

V1. Nicay' imbere ya Yesu, mpaboner' ihumure;
N' ahantu h' igikundiro; icyampa nkahibera.

Kumuhang' amaso ni byo bimpa gukiranuka.

V2. Kwicar' imbere ya Yesu, nta mahirw' arut' ayo;
Ni ho nsig' ibimbabaza, nkumva nduhutse rwose.
Iyo nicay' imbere ye, nkunda kumuganyira;
Na w' ababarana nanjye, maz' akampumuriza.

V3. Yesu mp' umugisha wawe; dore, ndategereje;
Ndeban' imbabazi zawe, menye k' unyitayeho.

165. Ndagukunda, Mwami
Written by T. Hastings

V1. Ndagukunda, Mwami; uzi ko ngukunda;

Ndagukunda Yesu, naw' urabizi;
Imirimo yanjy' izabyerekana.

V2. Nishimye, nishimye; rwose bitavugwa.
Ibyishimo byanjye, nta wabirondora.
Ndareb' ubutunzi buri mw' ijuru
Nzagabirwa nawe kubw' ubuntu bwawe.

V3. Yesu Mwami wanjye, ni we nkesha byose;
Ar' ugucungurwa, ari n' ubugingo.
Nzakogez' iteka, nkuririmbire,
Kuk' ubuntu bwawe bwandemy' umutima.

V4. Naguhwanya na nde, Mucunguzi wanjye?

V3. Yes' byo mfite byose, Nta mumaro bigira.

178. Ahar' Azaza Umusek' Utambitse

V1. Mu gihugu cyiza twasezeraniwe,
Hariy' ururembo rwera rw' hnana,
Tuzamuk' imisozi tunaniwe,
Tukarabukw' aho tuzab' iteka.

C. S. na A. : Tugeze hafi; Hafi y' iwacu,
Dore hararabagirana cyane,
Har' umucu' uturuka mu marembo,
Aho niho tuzab' iteka ryose,
Turirimbana n' abamarayika,
Turi haft yahoo
T. na B.: Tuge ... tugeze y' iwacu ... , Hafi y' iwacu,
Dore hararabagirana cyane,
Har' umucu' uturuka mu marembo,
Aho niho tuzab' iteka nJose,
Turirimbana n' abamarayika,
Turi, turi hafi ... ho.

V2. Mu bitabo by' abahanuzi tubwirwa,
Thy' umudugudu wera w' Imana,
N' inzira zaho zisizwe zahabu,
Amazu yahw' ararabagirana.

V3. Abazajyayo n' abizera bakeya,
Bakomez' amategeko y' Imana,
Tuzahora turangurur' amajwi,
Turirimb' indirimbo z' ibyishimo.

V4. Mbese tuzahurirayo bene Data,
Mu gihugu kirasirwa n' izuba?
Nimwemera ubutumwa bw' hnana,
Yesu n' aza azabahamagara.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

V1. Aha hantu har' amahoro, Kandi hari n' Umwuka Wera w' Uhoraho,
Kandi n' umuntu wese uhari, Afit' umunezero mwinshi bihebuje.

C. Mwuka Wera We, We numa nziza,
Ubane natwe, Utwuzuz' urukundo,
Turaguhimbaza kuk' uduhira,
Turataha tudashidikanya yuko duhiriwe twese.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

332. Nzabon' Umwami
Written by B. D. Ackley

V1. Nzabon' Umwami wanjy' aririmbirwa n' abamarayika
Tuzabana naw' iteka ryose mu gihugu cy' ibyiza.

C. Tuzahorana ibihe byose, Yankirije i Kalvari
Amaherezo nzabon' Umwami wanyitangiye kera

V2. Mur' icyo gihugu cyiza nta joro rizabay' ukundi.
Nzabana n' Umwami wancunguje amaraso y' akiza.

V3. Nzabana n' Umwami wanjye nkunda nzamureba mu maso,
Nzamuririmbira mushimira ubuntu yangiriye.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

V2. Garuka, Mukunzi garuka, Ntumwa nziza y' amahoro,
Nang' ibyaha byakubabaje, Bikantanya nawe.

V3. Mbega ngo ndagir' amahoro, Ntazigera nibagirwa!
Ariko byansizemw' imvun' itakungwa n' ab' isi.

V4. Icyo nagusimbuje cyose, Uko cyaba kiri kose,
Mfasha nitandukanye nacyo, Ngusenge wenyine.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

Written by J. W. Peterson

Ineza n' imbabazi ze nibyo bizanyomaho,
Iminsi yose nzaba ndiho.

Nzarira ku meza yanteguriye kera,
Ineza n' imbabazi ze nibyo bizanyomaho,
Iminsi yose nzaba ndiho.

342. Mukiza Wanjye Nyobora

C. S : Nzagukurikira hose,
Mukiza wanjye, Ngukurikire,
Nzagukurikira Mukiza unyobore.
A,T. na B. : Nzagukuriki ... , ... gukurikira hose,
Mukiza wanjye, Ngukurikire,
Nzagukuriki ... , ... rikira unyobore,
... za unyobore, nyobora.

V2. Mukiza wanjye, Nyobor' ah' ushaka,
Ukomez' undinde unampumurize,
N' ubw' umwijima wab' umbudits' imbere,
Ntabwo nzatiny' unyoboye Mukiza.

V3. Njyan' ah' ushaka Mwam' icyo ngusaba,
Nyuza mu nzira ntoya ne guteshuka,
Nubwo Satan' anyoshya anyongorera,
Mfasha njye nsubiza bwangu mpakana.

Ndi mu mabokw' akiza.

357. Ndishimye Pe! Yes’ Arankunda
Written by Philip P. Bliss

V1. Nishimiye ko Data wa twese, Yandikishij’ iby’ urukundo rwe.
Mu byanditswe muri Bibiliya, Nta cyaruta yuko Yes’ ankunda.

C. Ndishimye pe! Yes’ arankunda;
Arankunda, arankunda!
Ndishimye pe! Yes’ arankunda;
Anyakir’ uko ndi.

V2. Iyo nyobye maze ngateshuka, Ntabw’ ajy’ amvirira haba namba.
Angaruz’ ineza n’ urukundo, Nkamugarukira kukw’ ankunda.

C. Ndishimye pe! Yes’ arankunda;
Arankunda, arankunda!
Ndishimye pe! Yes’ arankunda;
Anyakir’ uko ndi.

V3. Ningera mu bwami bwo mw’ ijuru, Nzaririmb’ indirimbo z’ ikuzo.
Ariko cyane cyane nzishima, Ndirimb’ urukundo rw’ Umukiza.

C. Ndishimye pe! Yes’ arankunda;
Arankunda, arankunda!
Ndishimye pe! Yes’ arankunda;
Anyakir’ uko ndi.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

358. Yesu Yarampinduye Rwose!
Written byubrey H. Graham

V1. Nahoze ndindagira mu mwijima w’ ibyaha;
Maze Yes’ arambatura, none narahindutse;
Nd’ umwana w’ Imana rwos’ ubu, mfit’ amahoro.

C. Yarampinduye rwose, Anyigisha gusenga.
Nzasingiz’ urukundo Rwe!
Ubu yangiz’ uwe rwose;
Nahinduts’ umuntu mushya.

V2. Nahoze nd’ ikigenge, sinari nzi gusenga;
Yes’ araz’ arampindura, Yankunze bihebuje;
Arapfa kubwanjye; Ubu narihannye rwose.

C. Yarampinduye rwose, Anyigisha gusenga.
Nzasingiz’ urukundo Rwe!
Ubu yangiz’ uwe rwose;
Nahinduts’ umuntu mushya.

V3. Urukund’ umunezero n’ amahoro,
Ni byo byuzuy’ umutima wanjye!
Yesu yanyuzuyemw’ amp’ ubugingo bushya;
Nzibanira na w’ iteka.

C. Yarampinduye rwose, Anyigisha gusenga.
Nzasingiz’ urukundo Rwe!
Ubu yangiz’ uwe rwose;
Nahinduts’ umuntu mushya.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

359. Umucyo Uva Mw’ Ijuru
Written by Philip P. Bliss

V1. Umucyo uva mw’ ijuru, 
Uyobor’ abagenzi,
Uzadufasha tugere, 
Ku nkombe yo hakurya.

C. Mwami Yes’ umucyo waw’ umurikir’ abagenzi
Winjire mu nyanja, Maz’ ubakingir’ umuraba .

V2. Umwijim’ urabuditse, 
Inyanj’ irahorera;
Yes’ aduhozahw’ amas’ 
azadufasha twambuke.

C. Mwami Yes’ umucyo waw’ umurikir’ abagenzi
Winjire mu nyanja, Maz’ ubakingir’ umuraba .

V3. Mutyo ducan’ amatara, 
Dukomez’ urugendo.
Twe kuyobywa n’ abasare, 
Badafit’ urumuri.

C. Mwami Yes’ umucyo waw’ umurikir’ abagenzi
Winjire mu nyanja, Maz’ ubakingir’ umuraba.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

360. Wisubika Kwihana Nshuti
Written by Philip P. Bliss

V1. Wisubika kwihana nshuti;
Ni nko kubwir’ Umwuka Wera,
Ngo genda rwose, jye nzihan’ undi munsi.
Mbega ng’ uribuza amahirwe!

V2. Wisubika kwihana nshuti;
Dore Yes’ atez’ ibiganza.
Ihan’ uyu munsi, emer’ umusange;
Aguh’ ubugingo agukize.

V3. Wisubika kwihana nshuti;
Dor’ igihe kirarangiye.
Rwos’ igihe cy’ imbabazi kirashize,
Fatirana bwang’ usange Yesu.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

361. Ubuntu Butangaje!
Written by John Newton Wm Walter

V1. Mbeg’ ubuntu butangaje cyane!
Umutindi nkanjye gukizwa!
Ntabwo nabonaga, none ndabona.
Nakijijw’ ibyaha byanjye.

V2. N’ ubuntu bwanyerets’ aho nari;
Nari mu byaha byinshi cyane.
Kubw’ ubuntu Yesu yarandokoye;
Singifit’ ubwoba rwose.

V3. Navanywe mu kaga nari ndimo;
Mpagaze mu buntu bwa Yesu.
Kubw’ ubwo buntu nzager’ ibudapfa;
Mw’ ijuru kwa Data heza!

V4. Imyak’ igihumbi ndi mw’ ijuru;
Nzabanayo n’ Umwami Yesu.
Mbeg’ indirimbo nziza nzaririmba!
Nzaba nkeye cyane rwose.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

362. N’ Umutima Utuje
Written by H. Green

V1. N’ umutim’ utuje, nj’ imbere yawe;

V2. Nta rindi jwi nshaka kumva na gato;
Kerets’ ijwi ryawe, Yesu Mukiza.

V3. Amagambo yaw’ ambe mu mutima;
Yes’ ump’ ubugingo bw’ iteka ryose.

363. Yesu Mu Bugingo Bwanjye
Written by Thoro Harris

V1. Mbese har’ icyanezeza, Nko kubana na Yesu?
Nta cyanezeza nko kubana n’ uwo munyakuri.

C. Niba har’ ikinezeza,
Kurut’ ibindi byose;
Yesu mu bugingo bwanjye,
Rwos’ andutira byose

V2. Yitangiye kuncungura, Kubw’ ubuntu bw’ Imana.
Urukundo rwe rusumb’ ijuru n’ inyanja zose.

C. Niba har’ ikinezeza,
Kurut’ ibindi byose;
Yesu mu bugingo bwanjye,
Rwos’ andutira byose

V3. Ntacyo nshobora gukena, Mfit’ uwo Mucunguzi.
Ni w’ ump’ ibyo nkennye byose, Ni w’ unshoboza byose.

C. Niba har’ ikinezeza,
Kurut’ ibindi byose;
Yesu mu bugingo bwanjye,
Rwos’ andutira byose

V4. Ku mugez’ ubengerana, Nzaririmb’ indirimbo;
Ndi kumwe n’ abarokotse, Turirimbir’ Imana.

364 Nyir’ Ukwiringirwa Mana
Written by William M. Runyan 1925 (1870 – 1957)
V1. Nyir’ ukwiringirwa, Man’ Ihoraho,
Ntabw’ ubundikirwa n’ umwijima.
Ntuhinduka Mana yac’ idatsindwa;
Kand’ uhor’ uko wahoze Mana.

C. Nyir’ ukwiringirwa Mana ikomeye,
Ni wow’ uduh’ ibyo dukeneye.
Ikiganza cyawe, kitugabira,
Ibyo dukeneye buri munsi.

V2. Haba mu cyi cyangwa se mu muvumbi,
Inyenyeri, izuba n’ ukwezi,
Ibyo waremye byose Mana yacu,
Bihamya k’ ur’ Iman’ ikomeye.

C. Niba har’ ikinezeza,
Kurut’ ibindi byose;
Yesu mu bugingo bwanjye,
Rwos’ andutira byose

V3. Ugir’ imbabazi n’ impuhwe nyinshi.
Umunsi ku wund’ uraturinda.
Uduh’ ibyiringiro bikomeye;
By’ uko tuzabahw’ iteka ryose.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

366 Isoko Itemba
Written by R. Lowry

V1. Har’ isoko y’ ubunt’ isokw’ ihor’ itemba.

C. Iyo Soko, Ihora itemba;
Uyinywaho iramukiza.

V2. Ndumv’ ijwi ryongorera, Nk’ indirimbo nziza!
Rituruka mw’ isoko nziza idakama.
Ni yo soko y’ ubugingo, Ni y’ idukiz’ ubwihebe.

C. Iyo Soko, Ihora itemba;
Uyinywaho iramukiza.

V3. N’ isoko y’ umugisha, Itang’ ibyishimo.
N’ amaraso ya Yes’ akiz’ abanyabyaha.
N’ amaraso y’ Umukiza, Kand’ aratunganye rwose.

C. Iyo Soko, Ihora itemba;
Uyinywaho iramukiza.

V2. Mw’ Ijambo ryawe harimw’ umucyo, Tubonamw’ amasezerano.

C. Waduhaye Bibiliya Yera,

369. Ibyaha Byanjye Mbihaye Yesu
Written by Horatics Bomans, 1843 Justin H. Knecht and Edouard Husband

Byose ndabimwikoreje, Ngo mbon’ umudendezo.
Ibicumuro byanjye, Mbihay’ Umwami Yesu;
Anyejesh’ amaraso Ye, Anyeze nse n’ urubura.

V2. Kand’ ibyo nkennye byose, Mbishyize ku birenge Bye.
Yes’ akiz’ indwara zose, Ndetse n’ ibicumuro.
Intimba zanjye zose, Nzishyikiriza Yesu;
Kand’ imitwaro yanjye yose, Yes’ arayinyakira.

V3. Ndifuza kuba nka Yesu, Niyoroheje nka We.
Ndifuza kureba Yes’ Umwana w’ Imana Data.
Ndifuza kuzabana, Na Yes’ iyo mw’ ijuru;
Nkaririmbana n’ abera, Ntozwa n’ abamarayika.

370. Twegerej’ Igihe
Written by Holatius Bouas, 1844 Lowell Masson (1789 - 1872)

V1. Twegerej’ igihe cyo gutah’ iwacu;
Abacu twabuze tuzongera kubonana.
Mwami Yesu, Tegur’ ubugingo bwanjye;
Nyejesh’ amaraso yaw’ ankiz’ ibyaha byanjye.

V2. Dore duhanganye n’ imirab’ ikaze;
Arikw’ iri hafi kurangira bidatinze.
Tugiye kwiber’ ahatab’ amakuba;
Yesu nkiz’ ibyaha mbashe kuzager’ iwawe.

V3. Intugunda zose zigiye gushira.
Turi hafi guhanagurw’ amarira yose.
Mwami Yesu wamviriye amaraso.
Mfasha rwose, nzabe mur’ uwo muns’ uhiriwe.

V4. N’ igihe kigufi Yes’ akagaruka.
Yaradupfiriye, kugira ngo tuzabeho.
Mwami Yesu, Tegur’ ubugingo bwanjye;
Nyejesh’ amaraso yaw’ ankiz’ ibyaha byanjye.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

372. Kwa Kwizera Kw’ Abakurambere
Written by Henry F. Hamy, 1865 Frederick W. Faber, 1849 Alt by James G. Walton, 1871

V1. Kwa kwizera kw’ abakurambere, Kwa kundi kwababashishaga,
Kwemera kuzir’ akarengane; Kwicishw’ inkota n’ umuriro.

C. Uko kwizera natw’ ubu,
Tugufite mu mitima.
Tuzakunambaho rwose,
N’ iyo byaba ngombwa gupfa.

V2. Baraboshywe baranakubitwa, Baroshywe mu mazu y’ imbohe;

C. Uko kwizera natw’ ubu,
Tugufite mu mitima.

N’ iyo byaba ngombwa gupfa.

V3. N’ ubwo batotejwe bikomeye, Nta nzika bigeze bagira!

C. Uko kwizera natw’ ubu,
Tugufite mu mitima.
Tuzakunambaho rwose,

373. Tur’ Abagenzi
(Cantiques Populaires)

V1. Tur ‘ abagenzi mw’ iyi si, Twerekeje mw’ ijuru.
Yes’ araduhamagara, Ku nkombe ya yor’dani.
Yes’ uw’ uduhamagara, Arashaka ko tumusanga,
Tukabana mu bwiza bwe, Turirimb’ iteka.

C. Bizab’ umunezero kubana na Yesu,
Mu Bwami bwo mw’ ijuru, turirimb’ iteka.
Itorero Rye ryo mw’ ijuru, rizaririmb’ aleluya!
Rihimbaza Yes’ Umwami Mucunguzi wacu!

V2. Mbeg’ ukuntu bizaba byiza, Kumv’ amajwi meza;
Asingiz’ Umwana w’ Intam’ amajw’ atey’ ubwuzu!
Kand’ amajwi yac’ azab’ urwunge n’ ay’ abamarayika.
Twese tuzaririmbira Umwami w’ abami.

C. Bizab’ umunezero kubana na Yesu,
Mu Bwami bwo mw’ ijuru, turirimb’ iteka.
Itorero Rye ryo mw’ ijuru, rizaririmb’ aleluya!
Rihimbaza Yes’ Umwami Mucunguzi wacu!

V3. Abacunguwe na Kristo, Bazabon’ ubwiza bwe,
N’ abapfuye bamwizeye, Bazakangurwa na we.
Tuzasingiz’ intsinzi ye, Twese dukikij’ intebe ye.
Tuzataramana n’ Umwam’ atuganirize.

C. Bizab’ umunezero kubana na Yesu,
Mu Bwami bwo mw’ ijuru, turirimb’ iteka.
Itorero Rye ryo mw’ ijuru, rizaririmb’ aleluya!
Rihimbaza Yes’ Umwami Mucunguzi wacu!

V4. Dor’ umunsi w’ Uwiteka, Uri hafi kugera,
Kand’ abamwizeye twese, Tuzamusanganira.
Tuzasingiz’ urukundo, Rwatumye atang’ Umwana We,
Yesu Krist’ akadupfir’ akadukiz’ urupfu.

C. Bizab’ umunezero kubana na Yesu,
Mu Bwami bwo mw’ ijuru, turirimb’ iteka.
Itorero Rye ryo mw’ ijuru, rizaririmb’ aleluya!
Rihimbaza Yes’ Umwami Mucunguzi wacu!

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

378 Mwami Ha Umugisha Uru Rugo
Written by H. Plumhof

V1. Aba bashyingiwe, Bah’ umugisha wawe;

V3. Amahoro yawe, Atah’ urugo rwabo;

Yes’ ahore yonger’ urukundo rwabo.

Yes’ ubagumane, Mu maboko yawe.
Be guhungabanywa n’ imiraba y’ iyi si;

381. Mwami Nyir’ Isabato
Written byrr. From Frederick M. A. Venua, c. 1810

V1. Mwami Nyir’ isabato yera de! Nkez’ umunsi wawe w’ ikiruhuko.
Muns’ umpora ku mutima, N’ umuns’ ungarura mw’ intege;
Mpabwamw’ imigisha ngakomera.

V2. Munsi wuj’ amahoro n’ ituze, Umunsi wose numva nezerewe!
Intekerezo mbi zose, Zirahunga zikanjya kure;
Nkibwir’ ibyiza byera by’ ijuru.

V3. Mbeg’ ukunt’ ar’ iby’ igikundiro, Iyo ngeze mu munsi wahiriwe!
Nkumv’ indirimbo z’ ihozo, Ntwarwa gusa n’ ibyo mw’ ijuru!
Munsi mwiza mbonamw’ imigisha.

V4. Ntaramana nawe Mwami Yesu, Mur’ uyu munsi mwiza wahiriwe!
Jyew’ umugaragu wawe, Gukomez’ isabato yawe,
Bizampesha imigisha myinshi.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

382 Umubano Uba Mwiza
Written by Unknown

V1. Umubano uba mwiza, Mu rugo Yes’ arimo;
Urukundo ruranesha, Hab’ ituze rihamye.
Ikinyabupfura ni cyo kiranga urwo rugo,
Umugabo n’ umugore, Iyo bubah’ Imana.

V2. Urugo rwunguts’ umwana, Hab’ ibyishimo byinshi.
Nahabw’ uburere bwiza, Ab’ umwana w’ ijuru;
Umwan’ unezez’ Imana, Kand’ uzabana na yo;
Abane n’ Umwami Yesu, Kand’ ayoborwe na we.

V3. Urugo rwa hano mw’ isi, n’ urw’ igihe kigufi,
N’ ubund’ ibyo mw’ isi byose, Ntabwo biramba rwose.
Ibyiza birut’ ibindi, Kandi bizahoraho,
Tuzahurizwa mw’ ijuru; Tuzabana by’ iteka.

V4. Ibyo duhabwa n’ Imana mu rugendo turimo;
Tubyakiran’ ibyishimo, Tubyifatemo neza.
Twirinde gutsindwa n’ ibigeragezo by’ Umwanzi;
Dusarur’ iby’ urukundo, Rw’ Imana yac’ iduha.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

383. Mu Gihe Ntugarijwe
Written by D. A. R. Aufranc

V1. Mu gihe ntugarijwe N’ akaga gakomeye;
Yes’ umbwiz’ ijwi ryiz’ uti:
Humura ndahari.

V2. Iy’ umurab’ ukaramye, Ntabwo mpungabana.
Krist’ ankomez’ ambwir’ ati:
Humura ndahari.

V3. Umwijim’ iy’ ubuditse, Nkabur’ iyo ngana;
Numv’ ijwi rimpabura ngo:
Humura ndahari.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

384. Inyungu N’ Ibyubahiro …
Written bybagalatiya 8:14 W. B. Bradbury

V1. Inyungu n’ ibyubahiro byo mw’ iyi si, Jye ndabizinukwa.
Iyo ndeby’ umusaraba Yes’ Umwami yabambweho;
Nsang’ iby’ is’ ar’ impfabusa.

V2. Yesu yarababajwe cyane, Intimba imen’ umutima;
Kubw’ ubuntu yangiriye, N’ urukundo ruhanitse,
Rwamuteye kuncungura.

V3. Nari narazimiye rwose, Narabuze ibyiringiro;
Ancunguz’ amaraso ye, Nanjye mpabw’ icyubahiro;
Maz’ amahor’ aransāba.

V4. Urukundo rwawe rurera, Ruhoraho ibihe byose.
Nzahora ndwogez’ iteka, Kandi nzahora ndurata;
Sinzareka kuruvuga!

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

385. Munsi Mwiza W’ Umunezero
Written byhristopher Wordsworth Gesangbuch der Herzogel,(1807 - 1885) alt. Hofkapelle, 1784

V1. Munsi mwiza w’ umunezero! Ur’ umunsi wera de!
Ur’ umuns’ urut’ indi yose; Munsi wo kuruhukwa.
Abakomeye n’ aboroheje, Bunamir’ Uwiteka;
Baririmba: Wera! Wera! Wera! Uhimbazw’ iteka.

V2. Muns’ urinzwe cyane n’ Imana; nta cyawuhungabanya.
Tugomororerw’ amasoko yo muri Paradizo.
Soko y’ amariba mez’ afutse, Y’ amaz’ amar’ inyota.
Duhagarara kuri Pisiga, Tureb’ i Kanani.

V3. N’ umunsi tuzirikana cyan’ urukundo rw’ Imana;
Turushaho gutekereza ibyiza byo mw’ ijuru.
Duhabw’ imigisha myinshi cyane, Mur’ uyu munsi mwiza;
Twumva rwose twakwigumira, Mur’ uyu munsi wera!

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

386' Ibyaremwe Byose …
Written by Katherine K. Devis 1 Ngoma 16 : 23 Arr. By Wayne H. Hooper

V1. Ibyaremwe byose nibiter’ amajwi hejuru;
Byishimir’ Umuremyi, Bimuririmbire.
Koko yaraturemye; Kandi n’ Umurinzi wacu,
N’ Umuyobozi wacu, Kugez’ imperuka.
Adukingir’ ibihe byose, Atugend’ imber’ iteka.
Mu mwijim’ atuber’ inkingi y’ umuriro;
Atamurur’ ibihu; Akadukiz’ umwijima;
Tukagendera mu mucyo wera w’ Imana.

V2. Yahanits’ inyenyeri; Ategek’ izuba kuva.
Ni we wahanz’ imisozi, N’ inyanja zose;
Imigezi n’ inzuzi n’ amasoko birasuma!
Byose kw’ itegeko ry’ Umuremy’ udukunda.
Guhera mu bushorishori, No mu kuzimu mu nyanja;
Byose bihamy’ Imana, Yukw’ ar’ Umuremyi.
Natwe biradukwiye, Guhanik’ amajwi yacu;
Tugasingiz’ iyo Mana; tuti: Hozana!

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

387. Iyo Ngukoreye Yesu
Written by M. Russell

V1. Iyo ngukoreye Yesu, Biranezeza;
Iri turo ntuye, Mwami rikunezeze.

Bwakire Yesu
Kubw’ ubuntu bwawe Mwami,
Undind’ ibibi.

V2. Warancunguye Mukiza, Mb’ uwawe rwose.

C. Nguhay’ ubugingo bwanjye,
Bwakire Yesu
Kubw’ ubuntu bwawe Mwami,
Undind’ ibibi.

V3. Ungir’ umumarayika wihuta cyane;

C. Nguhay’ ubugingo bwanjye,
Bwakire Yesu
Kubw’ ubuntu bwawe Mwami,
Undind’ ibibi.

V4. Rwose kuzaba mw’ ijuru, Ni byo nifuza;
Nta byago nta n’ amakuba bizantezura.

C. Nguhay’ ubugingo bwanjye,
Bwakire Yesu
Kubw’ ubuntu bwawe Mwami,

388. Gihome Kidukingira
Written by Martin Luther, 1529

V1. Mana yac’ urakomeye; Gihome kidukingira;
Udukingir’ imiraba, Y’ ingorane n’ amakuba.
Uturind’ Umwanzi uhor’ aduhiga; Afit’ imbaraga,
Ntabwo twamwifasha; Ntitwamwibashisha na gato.

V2. Dushatse kwirwanirira, Twatsindwa rwose ruhemu.
Keretse dufite Yesu, We mukiranutsi wera.
Yaneshej’ umwanzi; Kandi yiteguye Kuturwanirira;
Turi kumwe na We; Nta kabuza tuzanesha.

V3. Iyi si yuzuy’ ibibi, Bishobora kuturimbura.
Ntidukwiye guhabuka; Twisung’ umucyo w’ Imana.
Ntiduterw’ ubwoba n’ Umwanzi w’ umucyo. Ni Se w’ umwijima;
Kand’ azarimburwa; Azajugunywa mu muriro!

V4. Nta wabasha guhindura ubushake bwa Rurema;
Ibyo yategetse byose, Ntibikomwa mu nkokora.
N’ ubwo byab’ urupfu, Cyangw’ ikindi cyose,
Ijambo ry’ Imana nta cyarivanaho, Kugez’ iteka n’ iteka.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

389 Ukomere Ub’ Intwari
Written by W. B. Bradbury and Philip P. Bliss
V1. Mukristo byuka, Yes’ aragushaka.
Ambar’ intwaro zose z’ urugamba;
Hangana n’ Umwanz’ udafit’ ubwoba;
Rwana; Shikama; Ntutiny’ urugamba.

C. Tyo shikama,
Ukomere ub’ intwari;
Utsind’ Umubisha.

V2. Rwanira Yesu, Ushyizeh’ umwete;
Kand’ ube maso kugez’ iherezo;
Ujy’ aho Yes’ akuyobora hose.
Rwana; Shikama; Ntutiny’ urugamba.

C. Tyo shikama,
Ukomere ub’ intwari;
Utsind’ Umubisha.

V3. Ntushidikanye Yesu n’ Umugaba.
Azakurinda; Azagukomeza,
Kand’ akuyoboresh’ urukundo rwe.
Rwana; Shikama; Ntutiny’ urugamba.

C. Tyo shikama,
Ukomere ub’ intwari;
Utsind’ Umubisha.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

390. Mbes’ Aho Tuzahurira Ku Cyambu?
Written by Horace L. Hastings Elitius S. Rice

V1. Mbes’ aho tuzahurira, Ku cyambu cya rwa ruzi,
Ahahor’ umucy’ iteka, Ntihab’ umubabaro?

C. Se koko tuzahurira hakurya y’ uruzi?
Tuzabonanirayo tuhanezererw’ iteka?

V2. Tuzahurira ku cyamb’ urugendo rurangiye?
Mbes’ aho tuzahurirayo, Maze twiruhutse?

C. Se koko tuzahurira hakurya y’ uruzi?
Tuzabonanirayo tuhanezererw’ iteka?

V3. Mbes’ aho twese tuzahurira mu mudugudu,
Wubatswe n’ Uhoraho, Urimbishijwe Yasipi?

C. Se koko tuzahurira hakurya y’ uruzi?
Tuzabonanirayo tuhanezererw’ iteka?

V4. Abacunguwe bose, Bazaririmb’ indirimbo;
Kand’ ibiremwa byose, Bizasingiz’ Uhoraho.

C. Se koko tuzahurira hakurya y’ uruzi?
Tuzabonanirayo tuhanezererw’ iteka?

V5. Mbes’ aho tuzabonana n’ abo twakundanaga?
Maze twumv’ amajwi yabo, Tubareba mu maso?

C. Se koko tuzahurira hakurya y’ uruzi?
Tuzabonanirayo tuhanezererw’ iteka?

V6. Mbese tuzabonana na Krist’ Umukiza wacu,
Aje kujyan’ intore ze, Mu bwami buhoraho?

C. Se koko tuzahurira hakurya y’ uruzi?
Tuzabonanirayo tuhanezererw’ iteka?

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

399. Yesu Nikoreye Umusaraba
Written by Henry F. Lyte Arr. From Mozart By Hubert P. Mason

V1. Yesu ndagukurikiye, Ndetse byose ndaje Mwami.
Nikorey’ umusaraba, Ndagukurikiye Mukiza.
Dor’ ibyar’ indamu zanjye, Sinkibyitayeho namba;
Mpisemo kugira Yesu, Akaba mu bugingo bwanjye.

V2. Ab’ isi barantoteza, Kuko badafite Yesu.
Batay’ Umukiza wanjye, Barashaka kungerageza.
N’ ubwo bampana bakandeka, Yesu ampor’ iruhande.
Yes’ ampa kwihanganira, Ingorane z’ iyi si zose.

V3. Isi yahaw’ agakiza, Yesu yarayicunguye.
Yesu yaneshej’ icyaha; Nta bwoba ngifite na gato.
Umwuka Wer’ ari muri twe; Mbeg’ umunezero mwinshi!
Nawe yaragupfiriye, Ng’ uzabane na we mw’ ijuru!

V4. Twar’ intwaro zo kwizera; Senga cyan’ ubudatuza;
Ugiye gutah’ ijuru, Hazab’ umunezero mwinshi!
Ibyo dukorera mw’ isi, Biri hafi kurangira.
N’ ibyiringiro bishyitse, Tuzabona Data mw’ ijuru.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

402. Mfat’ Ikiganza
Written by Thomas A. Dorsey

403 Mwami Wanjye Nyakira

Mpore nguhesh’ ikuzo.

V3. Mwami wanjye nguhay’ igihe cyanjye;

Mpore nguhesh’ ikuzo.

406. Kuba Mu Maboko Yawe
Written by James Mc Granahan

V1. Kuba mu maboko yawe, N’ iby’ igikundiro;
Man’ iyo nkumva bugufi, Numva nkomeye cyane.

C. S. na A.: Umwikorez’ amaganya, Umuh’ imitwaro yawe.
Muh’ ibikurushya byose, Kukw’ anezezwa no kukurinda.
T. na B.: Umwiko-re-ze, Korez’ amaganya,
Umuh’ i - h’imitwaro yawe.
Muh’ ibikuru - bikurushya byose,

Kunezezwa no kurinda.

N’ ubutayu n’ isi y’ igomero, Mw’ iyi si si hw’ iwacu.

428. Haguruka, Haguruka
Written by (Ancien Choral, 1704)

V1. Umwam’ araguhamagara haguruka.
Akuyobora mu mucyo, Mu nzira yo kwizera;
Mu rugendo rwo mw’ iyi si, Wigir’ ubwoba rwose;
Ngaho haguruka.

V2. Komera shikama b’ intwari ku rugamba;
N’ ubwo Satan’ atontoma, Yarangije gutsindwa;
Yesu yaramunesheje, Komez’ ibendera Rye;
Komera shikama.

V3. Komeza komeza, Rwanan’ ibyiringiro;
Ririmb’ indirimb’ igutera gushikama cyane.
Ntugashidikanye rwose, Gir’ umutim’ utuje;
Komez’ ukomere!

429. Intekerezo Zanjye Zibera Mw’ Ijuru
Written by Mme Henriksen - Laft

V1. Dor’ intekerezo zanjye zibera mw’ ijuru,
Ibyiringiro byanjye ni ho bituriza;
Mu mucyo w’ Uwiteka, Yes’ azaduhuriza;
Mw’ ijuru, ibudapfa ni ho tuzibera.

V2. Mw’ ijuru nta mibabaro, Tuzaba dutuje;
Tuzahanagurw’ amarira tugezeyo.
Nta rupfu ruzabayo, nta kiduhungabanya;
Tuzabana by’ iteka, Turi mu mahoro.

V3. Mbeg’ ukuntu tuzishima, Twongeye guhura,
N’ abo twari twaratandukanijwe kera!
Mw’ iteraniro ryiza, Maze duhoberane,
Twibere mu byishimo bitazahinduka.

V4. Mbeg’ inanga z’ izahabu zizacurangwayo!
Ubw’ abacunguwe bazaba bateranye.
Yes’ azatuzamura, Atugeze mw’ ijuru,
Dusingiz’ urukundo, Twakunzwe n’ Imana.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

430. Nabara Nte Uburyo Yesu Yapfuye?
Arr. By John Bernard

V1. Nabara nte uburyo Yesu yapfuye? Uw’ abamarayika baramya!
N’ Umwunger’ ushak’ uwari wazimiye, Ngw’ amucyur’ agaruke mu rugo.
Se ntiyabyawe n’ umukobwa Mariya, Mu muvure i Betelehemu!
Kandi se ntiyakuriy’ i Nazareti! Ng’ uk’ uko yaje hano mw’ isi y’ ibyaha!

V2. Mvuge nt’ uko yababajw’ akituriza! Agakiz’ iyi si y’ amarira;
N’ umutim’ umenetse ku musaraba, Yesu yambitsw’ ikamba ry’ amahwa!
Ni w’ ukiza ab’ imitim’ imenetse, Kand’ akiz’ ubwob’ umunyabyaha!
Adukiz’ imitwaro yose y’ ibyaha, N’ ub’ ari hano rwos’ ari kumwe natwe.

V3. Nabara nte uko yireherejeho amahanga yose yo mw’ iyi si!
Yahaw’ ubutware mw’ isi no mw’ ijuru, Nta na hamwe Yes’ atar’ Umwami.
Ari hafi kugaruka mu bwiza bwe, Kand’ amaso yos’ azamubona;
Azab’ aje kujyan’ abe bamwizeye; Babane mu bwiza burabagirana!

V4. Nabara nte ukw’ isi yos’ imuramya! Ukw’ acyah’ umurab’ ugahunga!
Niw’ ushyir’ umunezero mu mitima, Kubw’ urukundo rwe rutangaje!
Mwa bari mw’ isi mwe, ni mumuhimbaze, Amajw’ ibihumb’ amusingize!
Ijuru ni rihamy’ icyubahiro cye; Yukw’ ar’ Umwami n’ Umucunguzi w’ isi.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

Tunezerwe twishime.

V4. Dukurikiz’ inama nziza, Tub’ abantu beza b’ intwari;

433. Nyenyeri Yo Mu Ruturuturu
Written by. H. Purday

V1. Nyenyeri yo mu ruturuturu unyobore;
Igih’ inzir’ icuz’ umwijima unyobore.
Umfash’ ukubok’ ukanyobora,
Mbese nabur’ ibyiringiro nte?

V2. Jye ntabwo nagushidikanyaho unyobore;
Umpumure maze mbon’ inzira unyobora.
Natinze rwose kukuyoboza,
Ubu ndaje noneho nyobora.

V3. Mu bihanamanga mu bitare unyobore;
Mu bishanga ndetse no mu bihu unyobore.
Ndashaka kumv’ ijwi ryawe Yesu;
We Muyobozi mwiz’ utayobya.

V4. Mu gihe ntentebutse mbabaye unyobore;
Ndi mu cyunamo nabuz’ abanjye unyobore.
Nzi k’ undeba nez’ uri mw’ ijuru;
Ntey’ intambwe ngusang’ unyobore.

V5. Kubw’ urukundo rwawe, Mukiza unyobore;
Ndakwiyeguriye Mwami mwiza unyobore.
Yesu wabambwe ku musaraba,
Muri byose komez’ unyobore.

446. Mwami W’ Amahanga Yose

V3. Mwami ngusaby’ imbabazi, Nataniye mu bwanganyi;
Mfasha menye ibyaha byanjye, Ne kukubamb’ ubwa kabiri.

V4. Mbashisha kuvuganira, Abanyantege nke bose,
Barenganwa ntibitabweho; Mpa gushikama mbavugire.

V5. Unyuzuz’ Umwuka Wera, Mbashe gukor’ ibikwiye,
Aho mba hos’ igihe cyose, Nkorah’ unkoresh’ ibikwiye.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

449 Dusingize Yesu Nyir’ Ukunesha
Written by Martial J. Mercer

V1. Dusingize Yesu Nyir’ ukunesha!

Tuzirikan’ urukundo rwa Yesu.
Kand’ urukundo rwe rurahanitse,
Ubwami bw’ Imana buri muri twe.

V2. Kand’ isi yac’ igez’ ahakomeye,
Dor’ amahoro rwos’ ayishizemo.
Is’ ikeney’ umucy’ uva mw’ ijuru,
Tuyerek’ Umukiza Emanweli.
Bwoko bw’ Imana nitwitange rwose,
Tuvug’ ubutumwa twitange rwose.

V3. Tujy’ ahantu hose tubabwirize,
Hirya hino hakeney’ ubutumwa.
Benshi ntacyo bazi cyo gucungurwa,
Bakwiriye kubwirw’ iby’ agakiza;
Bakameny’ ibyo gucungurwa kwabo.
Nimutyo dutwaze tubagereho.

V4. Abavugabutumwa bakeneye,
Amasengesho n’ urukundo rwinshi.
Tubazirikane tubasabire,
Tubashyigikire, tubakomeze.
Yes’ agiye kuza mu cyubahiro,
Twe kugir’ ubwoba tub’ abaneshi.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

C. Sop: Ijwi numva, Rinter’ ibyiringiro;

Rinter’ ibyi – byishimo pe!
…shimo mu mutima.

Rintera ibyiri – byiringiro;
Rinter’ ibyi – byishimo pe!
…shimo mu muti… mu mutima.

V3. Ibyo byiringiro bitsika mu mutima wanjye;
Bitamurur’ umwijima, Umucy’ ugatangaza!
Iy’ Umwami yimye mu mutima waw’ ushavuye,
Ibyiringiro bishyitse biguma mu mutima.

456. Yes’ Arankunda

Urukundo rutadohoka.
Ampaz’ umunezero mwinshi,
Arankunda!

V3. Mu minsi mib’ arandengera,
Akandwanaho mu makuba.
Andokora mu byago byose,
Arankunda!

Bikayonga bigashiraho.
Arik’ urukundo rwa Yesu,
Ruhoraho.

V5. Yaryamishijwe mu muvure,

Ni jye yagiriraga rwose,
Arankunda.

V6. Kand’ azagaruka mu bicu,

Mu ndirimbo.

471 Yes’ Uradukunda!
Written by. H. Urhan

V1. Yes’ uradukunda nka Data wa twese,
Kand’ urukundo rwawe, Ruradukomeza,
Iy’ imitim’ itentebutse.
Amaraso yawe urayatwejesha; Kubw’ urukundo rwawe,
Wemeye kwitanga; Ni twe wagiriraga Mwami.

V2. Ugiye kugenda wasiz’ uvuz’ uti:
“Muzajye mukundana nk’ uko nabakunze.”
Nta wakunda nkawe Mwami we!
Duhe gukundana, Nk’uko wadukunze; Uduhe gufatanya,
Bitum’ is’ imenya, Y’ uko tur’ abana ba Yesu.

V3. Mbe, Mwami mwiza we! N’ iby’ igikundiro,
Y’ uko tugukorera, Dusengera hamwe,
Twita no ku nshingano zacu.
Twite ku murimo; Tuzi neza y’ uko uduhora bugufi,
Ukatubashisha gutungany’ inshingano zacu.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

472 Nje Kugushima
Written by Harmony by Johanna Wagener

V1. Nje kugushima Mwami Mana, Nkuzaniy’ ishimwe ryanjye;
N’ ubw’ umwijima wabudika, Wow’ uramboneshereza.
Wangiz’ umwana wawe Mana, Unyitaho buri munsi;
Ni wowe soko y’ imigisha, Ngushimiy’ imigish’ umpa.

V2. Ngushimira k’ uhor’ undinda, N’ ukuboko kwawe Mana.
Iy’ umutim’ ucits’ intege, Unsubizamw’ imbaraga;
Iyo nabuze kivurira, Undwanah’ ukanduhura;
Dor’ ukuboko kw’ Uwiteka, Ntikwananiwe gukiza.

V3. Ngushimiy’ impuhw’ ungirira, Unkurahw’ ibicumuro.
Iy’ utambabarir’ ibyaha, Nari guhungira he se?
Data ntabwo nzagutenguha, Warankijije ndakira.
Mu maraso y’ Umwami Yesu, Ni ho mboner’ agakiza.

V4. Nzi neza rwos’ uwo nizeye, Ni we umboneshereza;
Ni we Gitare kinkingira, Ni we byiringiro byanjye;
Kabone n’ ubwo nacogozwa, Ntazabura kunyitaho.
Yampay’ ubugingo bw’ iteka, Nzajya mushimir’ iteka.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

495. Ntabwo Nzaguhāna
Written by Unknown

V1. Ntabwo nzaguhāna sinzakureka, Sinzagutererana na hato;
Nzahora nkurinda, nzajya nkurengera, Nzubahirish’ izina ryanjye,
Nd’ Uwiteka ntugir’ ubwoba, Umvira gus’ iby’ Iman’ ivuga.

V2. Umurab’ usheze nugotwa n’ ibyago, Utabaz’ Imana usenge,
Izakubumbatiz’ amaboko yayo, Kand’ izakurind’ ikwiteho,
Mu bishuko nugeragezwa, Iman’ izajy’ ikwerek’ inzira.

V3. Nuhabw’ imigisha iva mw’ ijuru, Menya yukw’ Iman’ ikuba hafi,
Niwumva wishimye ufit’ amahoro, iyo byose bigenda neza,
Uwiteka ntazakureka, Azajy’ arinda intambwe zawe.

V4. Igih’ ubugingo bugoswe n’ ijoro, nugotwa n’ ibicu komera.
Uwitek’ azajya akumurikira, azakuyobora mu mucyo!
Humur’ urukundo rw’ Imana, Ntabwo ruzigera rukuvaho.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

496. Ndakwihaye
Written by J. H.

V1. Ndakwihaye ndakwiyeguriy’ ubu, Nkwishyize mu maboko unkoreshe!
Mber’ ingabo undinde abashaka gutuma ndeka kwizera kwanjye.

C. Yesu yarankijije kubw’ ubuntu;
Yes’ Umwami yameney’ amaraso;
Ndi hafi ye, na w’ ampora bugufi;
Ijwi rye rirankomeza cyane.

V2. Ndakwihaye umbabarir’ ibyaha, Bimveho ntibizongere kwibukwa;
Muri Yesu byose bibe bishyashya, Uranyeze Mwami nere rwose.

C. Yesu yarankijije kubw’ ubuntu;
Yes’ Umwami yameney’ amaraso;
Ndi hafi ye, na w’ ampora bugufi;
Ijwi rye rirankomeza cyane.

V3. Nguhay’ impagarike n’ ubugingo, Sinkiri uwanjye ngira umwe nawe!
Unyuzuz’ umuriro wawe waka, Maze nkugarurir’ inzimizi.

C. Yesu yarankijije kubw’ ubuntu;
Yes’ Umwami yameney’ amaraso;
Ndi hafi ye, na w’ ampora bugufi;
Ijwi rye rirankomeza cyane.

V4. Mwam’ utagereranywa ndakwihaye, Mbese nakwanga nte kugukorera?
Nubwo twasakirana n’ ibirushya, Ntuzajy’ ubura kuturengera.

C. Yesu yarankijije kubw’ ubuntu;
Yes’ Umwami yameney’ amaraso;
Ndi hafi ye, na w’ ampora bugufi;
Ijwi rye rirankomeza cyane.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

497. Nzogera Murangurure
Written by S. W. Martin

V1. Nzogera murangurure, Mutangaz’ ubutumwa!
Mu byaro mu mijyi hose, Humvikan’ indirimbo.
Dor’ Imana yakunz’ isi, Yatanz’ Umwana wayo,
Aza mw’ isi kudupfira, Is’ ishim’ iyo Mana.

C. Sop.: Nimurangurure, Muvug’ iby’ amahoro!
Nimurangurure, Nimuvug’ iby’ agakiza!
A. T. na B.: Nimura-ngurure, Muvug’ iby’ amahoro!
Nimura-ngurure, Muvuge i - gakiza!

V2. Nzogera nimutangaze ivuka ry’ Umukiza;
Kubw’ ineza yagiriye umunyabyaha wese.
Mubivug’ ahantu hose, N’ inkuru y’ imbabazi.
Ijuru n’ isi nibyamamaz’ iyo neza nyinshi.

C. Sop.: Nimurangurure, Muvug’ iby’ amahoro!
Nimurangurure, Nimuvug’ iby’ agakiza!
A. T. na B.: Nimura-ngurure, Muvug’ iby’ amahoro!
Nimura-ngurure, Muvuge i - gakiza!

V3. Mureb’ Umukiza Yesu, Mureb’ asuzugurwa,
Kand’ ar’ Umwana w’ Imana, Tukabon’ agakiza.
Yaducunguj’ amaraso ye y’ igiciro cyinshi;
Turangurure tuvuge iby’ uko gucungurwa.

C. Sop.: Nimurangurure, Muvug’ iby’ amahoro!
Nimurangurure, Nimuvug’ iby’ agakiza!
A. T. na B.: Nimura-ngurure, Muvug’ iby’ amahoro!
Nimura-ngurure, Muvuge i - gakiza!

V4. Nimugende mujye hose, Mugere mw’ isi yose;
Mwingingir’ abigometse, Bagarukir’ Imana.
Dore bari mu makuba, Bakeney’ agakiza;
Bemer’ Umukiza Yesu, Abah’ umudendezo!

C. Sop.: Nimurangurure, Muvug’ iby’ amahoro!
Nimurangurure, Nimuvug’ iby’ agakiza!
A. T. na B.: Nimura-ngurure, Muvug’ iby’ amahoro!
Nimura-ngurure, Muvuge i - gakiza!

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

498. Muze Dusingiz’ Umwami Wacu
Written by J. MacGranahan

V1. Muze dusingiz’ Umwami wacu, Wadukunze bitarondoreka!
Kumumenya bituma dutuza, Dore ni we Mwungeri wacu!

C. S. na A.: Dusingiz’ Umucunguzi,
Yes’ Umwami, Nyir’ ukunesha!
Yaduhaye ibyishimo,
N’ imigisha yo mw’ ijuru
T. na B. : Dusingiz’ Umucunguzi, Mucunguz’ Umwami wacu,
Yes’ Umwami, Yes’ Umwami, Nyir’ u(ku)nesha, ukunesha!
Yaduhaye – yaduhaye ibyishimo – ibyishimo,
N’ imigisha – n’ imigisha yo mw’ ijuru – yo mw’ ijuru.

V2. Mu byaha ndetse no mu bujiji, Tutizera nta byiringiro;
Yameny’ ibyacu aratwegera, Maz’ adukiz’ imibabaro.

C. S. na A.: Dusingiz’ Umucunguzi,
Yes’ Umwami, Nyir’ ukunesha!
Yaduhaye ibyishimo,
N’ imigisha yo mw’ ijuru
T. na B. : Dusingiz’ Umucunguzi, Mucunguz’ Umwami wacu,
Yes’ Umwami, Yes’ Umwami, Nyir’ u(ku)nesha, ukunesha!
Yaduhaye – yaduhaye ibyishimo – ibyishimo,
N’ imigisha – n’ imigisha yo mw’ ijuru – yo mw’ ijuru.

V3. Yamurikiy’ imitima yacu, Tumenya nez’ ukuri kwera!
Maz’ uwo Mwam’ ab’ Umuvandimwe; Yatuberey’ Umucunguzi.

C. S. na A.: Dusingiz’ Umucunguzi,
Yes’ Umwami, Nyir’ ukunesha!
Yaduhaye ibyishimo,
N’ imigisha yo mw’ ijuru
T. na B. : Dusingiz’ Umucunguzi, Mucunguz’ Umwami wacu,
Yes’ Umwami, Yes’ Umwami, Nyir’ u(ku)nesha, ukunesha!
Yaduhaye – yaduhaye ibyishimo – ibyishimo,
N’ imigisha – n’ imigisha yo mw’ ijuru – yo mw’ ijuru.

V4. Ubu ntitugitwarwa n’ ubwoba, Kuko yaduciriy’ akanzu;
Duhore dutez’ ijwi Ry’ amatwi, Ntabwo tuzigera tuyoba.

C. S. na A.: Dusingiz’ Umucunguzi,
Yes’ Umwami, Nyir’ ukunesha!
Yaduhaye ibyishimo,
N’ imigisha yo mw’ ijuru
T. na B. : Dusingiz’ Umucunguzi, Mucunguz’ Umwami wacu,
Yes’ Umwami, Yes’ Umwami, Nyir’ u(ku)nesha, ukunesha!
Yaduhaye – yaduhaye ibyishimo – ibyishimo,
N’ imigisha – n’ imigisha yo mw’ ijuru – yo mw’ ijuru.

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

499. Duhimbaze Yes’ Umucunguzi!
Written byanny J. Crosby Zaburi 146 : 2 Chester G. Allen

V1. Duhimbaze Yes’ Umucunguzi wacu, Twamamaze twes’ urukundo rwe!
Afit’ icyubahiro giheranije, Izina rye ryera niryubahwe!
Nk’ uk’ umwungeri arind’ umukumbi we, Ni ko Yesu arind’ abana be!
Duhimbaze Yes’ Umucunguzi wacu, Twamamaze twes’ urukundo rwe!

V2. Duhimbaze Yes’ Umucunguzi wacu, Watubabarijw’ akadupfira!
Ni we Gitare cy’ ibyiringiro byacu, By’ agakiza gahorahw’ iteka.
Yikorey’ imibabaro yacu yose, Kubw’ urukundo rwe rwinshi cyane.
Duhimbaze Yes’ Umucunguzi wacu, Watubabarijw’ akadupfira!

V3. Duhimbaze Yes’ Umucunguzi mwiza, Mw’ ijur’ indirimbo zihanikwe!
Yaranesheje rwose yambay’ ikamba, N’ Umutware Nyir’ icyubahiro!
Dor’ agiye kugaruka bidatinze, Abengerana mu cyubahiro.
Duhimbaze Yes’ Umucunguzi mwiza, Mw’ ijur’ indirimbo zihanikwe!

© 2011 Rwanda Union Mission of The Seventh-day Adventists

500. Ku Marembo Y’ Ijuru
Written byrr. by I. G. Martin

V1. Tuzahura mu gitondo, Ku marembo y’ ijuru;
B’ umugenzi wo kwizerwa, Utazakerererwa.

C. Sop. : Tuzahura mu gitondo,
Duhurire kw’ irembo ry’ ijuru.
Tuzahura mu gitondo,
Duhurire mw’ ijuru mu byishimo.
A., T. na B. : Tuzahura mu gitondo, Mu gitondo, mu gitondo,
Duhurire kw’ irembo ry’ ijuru (ry’ ijuru).
Tuzahura mu gitondo, Mu gitondo, mu gitondo,
Duhurire mw’ ijuru mu byishimo.

V2. Nimutebutse kuza kwe, Mwe gutinda mu nzira;
Dor’ araza mu gitondo, Aradutegereje.

C. Sop. : Tuzahura mu gitondo,
Duhurire kw’ irembo ry’ ijuru.
Tuzahura mu gitondo,
Duhurire mw’ ijuru mu byishimo.
A., T. na B. : Tuzahura mu gitondo, Mu gitondo, mu gitondo,
Duhurire kw’ irembo ry’ ijuru (ry’ ijuru).
Tuzahura mu gitondo, Mu gitondo, mu gitondo,
Duhurire mw’ ijuru mu byishimo.

V3. Rek’ umucyo wawe wake, Yes’ arategereje.
Tuzabana na w’ iteka, Mw’ iteraniro ryiza!

C. Sop. : Tuzahura mu gitondo,
Duhurire kw’ irembo ry’ ijuru.
Tuzahura mu gitondo,
Duhurire mw’ ijuru mu byishimo.
A., T. na B. : Tuzahura mu gitondo, Mu gitondo, mu gitondo,
Duhurire kw’ irembo ry’ ijuru (ry’ ijuru).
Tuzahura mu gitondo, Mu gitondo, mu gitondo,
Duhurire mw’ ijuru mu byishimo.

V4. Naza n’ ibyishimo byinshi, Ku marembo y’ ijuru;
Mbeg’ iteraniro ryiza, Turi kumwe n’ abera!

C. Sop. : Tuzahura mu gitondo,
Duhurire kw’ irembo ry’ ijuru.
Tuzahura mu gitondo,
Duhurire mw’ ijuru mu byishimo.
A., T. na B. : Tuzahura mu gitondo, Mu gitondo, mu gitondo,
Duhurire kw’ irembo ry’ ijuru (ry’ ijuru).
Tuzahura mu gitondo, Mu gitondo, mu gitondo,
Duhurire mw’ ijuru mu byishimo.
